Have the chance to maximize your page speed insights and achieve high Core Web Vitals and higher SEO rankings.\n137\t\n138\t- Loads the smallest file size possible of CSS and JS files in the frontend, ~ only 7.8kb total\n139\t- Adds almost no PHP server overhead for fast page loads\n140\t- Zero Bloat, no jQuery, no dependencies\n141\t- Optimized page loading with focus on Core Web Vitals\n142\t- Responsive image loading for faster browsing speeds in mobile devices\n143\t- Compatible with Optimization Plugins and use optimization techniques such as combining CSS and JS files and minification\n144\t\n145\t## Integrations & Compatibility\n146\t\n147\tMake your page building experience more well-rounded by using other popular tools.
